However, when I took a taxi back to the hotel during the day, no one opened the door. The staff at the door Just watching you get off the bus, and when I left the store, no one helped me carry my luggage, not even a simple inquiry, because my luggage was very big and conspicuous.
2. When checking in, the front desk did not introduce me to any facilities and equipment of the hotel, including breakfast time, restaurant location, and elevator location. I asked myself all of them. It was really just a simple check-in. , help me check in on the system
3. During my stay at the hotel, I called and asked about the hotel restaurant. The staff who answered the question didn't know the restaurant's business hours and the prices of the dishes. It was very unprofessional. There were also staff members who saw me and didn't say hello but just looked at me. gone
4. There was only one restaurant on the sign on the elevator. Later, I entered by mistake and found out that there was a Chinese restaurant on the 7th floor. It was quite magical.
5. There are no hotel bags in the room. I want to pack some things and I have to go to the front desk to ask about the bags.
6. When I was having breakfast, I saw a customer asking the staff if he could get her a cup of soy milk. The staff said, "We are self-service and you can get the soy milk over there." That's it, it's purely self-service. What else do I need from you? I also know that it is self-service, but I just want a cup of soy milk. Can't we provide this kind of service? Now that I think about it, I find it quite funny.
7. It is also interesting to call the hotel front desk to ask about the check-in experience. They just ask directly without guiding the guests. For example, what are the hotel facilities and equipment? Ingredients? service quality? If there is no guidance, what should the guests say?
Final summary:
The hotel has not properly trained its employees on predictive services. What is predictability? Elementary predictability: When I am eating, if I wave my hand, you will know that I need a glass of water. Advanced foresight: When I was about to wave to you, you had already brought me the water.
